tetex-fonts

  • Summary: The font files for the TeX text formatting system.
  • URL: http://www.tug.org/teTeX/
  • Version: 1.0.6
  • Release: 1
  • Group: Applications/Publishing
  • License: distributable
  • Installation size: 18,305,482 bytes
  • Operating system: freemint
  • Provides:
    • tetex-fonts = 1.0.6-1
  • Requires:
    • /bin/sh
  • Conflicts:
    • (none)
  • Relocations: (none)
  • Build date: Fri Feb 4 01:30:06 2000 UTC
  • Upload date: Fri Feb 4 02:11:06 2000 UTC
  • Packager: Frank Naumann (fnaumann(at)freemint.de)
  • Vendor: Sparemint
  • Sources: tetex-1.0.6-1.src.rpm (50,902,928 bytes)
  • Last change: Frank Naumann <fnaumann@cs.uni-magdeburg.de> Sun Nov 28 10:00:00 1999 UTC
    - updated to 1.0.6
    - adpated all Redhat changes
  • Description:
    The tetex-fonts package contains fonts used by both the Xdvi previewer and
    the TeX text formatting system.


    You will need to install tetex-fonts if you wish to use either tetex-xdvi
    (for previewing .dvi files in X) or the tetex package (the core of the TeX
    text formatting system).
